Mr. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Preface
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The Ideal World for God and Humanity
I would like to express my gratitude once again to all the ladies and gentlemen who have attended this evening. I mentioned yesterday that I have long awaited the opportunity to meet the American people, and I am grateful to meet those of you who are here for the first time today. The topic I would like to discuss with you today is "The Ideal World for God and Humanity or the Unified World," and I will speak on this subject.

Where should we begin to pursue the ideal world (the unified world)?
All of humanity living in the world today hopes that we could become one world, or an ideal world, in our hearts. However, no matter how much we think about it, it seems that there is no possibility of that happening at this time, and this is a sorrow that you all understand well. 
If God exists, it is certain that, like us humans, God would also desire such an ideal world or one world. What both God and humanity desire is undoubtedly one world and an ideal world. If there is an all-powerful God, then He must inevitably establish such a world. 
February 4, 1972 (Friday), Lincoln Center (New York, USA).
* This speech was given during a public lecture tour of seven major cities in the United States and was also published in the April 1972 issue of <Unified World>.
The Ideal World for God and Humanity
If there are people who know God's power or believe in God, they will think that this matter must be accomplished. 
Humans desire a world of peace and a unified world, but they all acknowledge that this world, as it is, cannot become one. The democratic world wishes to unify the world from its own standpoint, while the communist world wishes to do so from its own. This is the reality. 
So, can the communist world unite with the democratic world, or can the democratic world unite with the communist world? When we look at this issue, it is an extremely difficult problem. 
The democratic world worships one God, while the communist world denies the existence of God and worships materialism. Even if the communist world worships materialism, if they acknowledge the existence of God, there might be a possibility, but they deny His existence. If there is a God and materialists claim there is none, then the enemy before that God must be the communists, that is, the materialists. 
When do you think this struggle will end? As long as this struggle continues, a unified world or an ideal world of peace cannot come. So before we seek unity centered on the world and pursue the ideal world, is there a country that can be considered a unified nation or a country that can represent the ideal world? That is also not possible. 
Before there can be a unified world, there must be a unified nation, and before there can be a unified nation, there must be a unified race; before there can be a unified race, there must be a unified family, and before there can be a unified family, there must be a unified individual. This is the problem. So where should we start with unity? Since this world is a world of results, we must conclude that we cannot start from the world of results but must seek from the individual, who is the cause. 
Humans are both the embodiment of good and the embodiment of evil.
As I mentioned last night, we individuals have become humans with two opposing purposes. This is something no one can deny. The heart wishes to go toward goodness, but the body urges it to go in the opposite direction. I am undoubtedly a being formed by the union of heart and body, yet these two are in conflict. 
Such individuals, that is, such men and women, come together to form families. However, because there is an inner person and an outer person, when two couples meet, they behave as four separate individuals. If there are eight members in a family, those eight members become a family that behaves like sixteen individuals with opposing directions. When viewed from the perspective of one family, families stand in opposing positions to each other. In this way, whether it is a clan, a race, a nation, or the world, divisions occur. 
However, the fortunate thing is that they have not divided into hundreds or thousands of branches but rather into two major ones. This is what is strange. 
If God exists, He cannot simply abandon such humans, so He must be working behind the scenes of history, which we humans do not know. If there is a God, there is also Satan, who drives humanity toward evil, and Satan tries to lead in the opposite direction of God's guidance. 
However, no matter how much Satan opposes the absolute God, he has no authority to oppose the principles established by God. What is right is managed by God, and what is bad is managed by Satan. The question is where the results of this battle between God and Satan will lead. This will certainly apply to the world, but it starts from the individual. Therefore, we must understand that we humans can become the embodiment of evil or the embodiment of good. In other words, we must recognize that a person can be both the starting point of good and the starting point of evil. 
Everyone, rising symbolizes goodness, while descending signifies badness. When you have something to be praised for in front of people, you want to show it off. When you realize you have done something bad, you want to hide away. 
When doing good, you can promote it and shout to the world to follow your example. When doing bad, you try to hide it for fear of being discovered. No one who has committed a crime, such as theft, walks around proudly promoting it. They do so in secret. 
We must recognize that within us, there are two parts: one that desires to rise and another that desires to fall. What is it that desires to rise? It is the action of conscience. What desires to fall? It is the attitude of "I can do whatever I want, regardless of conscience." There is no merchant or great person who commits evil without feeling the pain of conscience. Our conscience is the dwelling place of God, while our bodies are the dwelling place of Satan; the conscience is the origin of heaven, and the body is the origin of hell. 
Therefore, when we look at the nature of good and evil, we can see that they are fundamentally different. Good seeks the benefit of the whole, while evil denies the whole and seeks only for oneself. To an evil person, there is no family, no relatives, no nation, and no world. In contrast, a good person seeks to prioritize family over self, community over family, nation over community, and the world over the nation. 
Until now, history has been woven around the struggle between self-interest and public interest. When God looks at this world, it is an absolute requirement to destroy the foundation of evil centered on the body. Conversely, the demand of evil centered on Satan is to ruthlessly destroy conscience and everything associated with it. 
This is how history has been woven through struggle. We can conclude that humanity in this world is inevitably divided between materialism and idealism, with God's side prioritizing conscience and evil's side prioritizing the body, denying God's existence and focusing solely on materialism. If there were no God, such a world of results could not exist. Evil emphasizes jealousy, division, and conflict, leading to self-destruction. 
When we look at it this way, where should ideals and unity begin? Ultimately, it must start with "me." At the root, it is us. It is the individual. Since what God desires is a world of unity and an ideal world, humanity should also desire that, but since humans are not in that state, there must be teachings or methods to instruct humanity on how to achieve unity. 
Teachings of Religion
Do you want to know that method? It is not the method you desire. It is not a method anyone desires. First, it is to strike against what opposes your conscience. God cannot strike it for you. If God could strike it, then Satan could strike it too. People are caught in the middle, fighting over what is taken. I will discuss the specifics of this later due to time constraints. 
Therefore, God's teaching is to focus on conscience and say, "Strike! Strike! Strike!" regarding the body. This movement must be carried out globally. It is to do what the body dislikes. The institution that teaches this, as I mentioned last night, is religion. 
So what does the teaching of religion say? It says, "Strike the body! Do not eat what you want! Do not do what you want! Do not do what the body desires!" It teaches to deny everything; any high-level religion teaches this. Buddhism emphasizes asceticism as an important teaching. Christianity has sacrifice as its motto. If any religion does not teach this, it cannot be considered a religion. This is one method. 
To practice this as it is, it is extremely difficult for humans, so God must think that He cannot just leave it as it is and must present a way to achieve unity. Because the strength of the human body and mind is similar, the standard fluctuates back and forth. If the body and mind are in a 5 to 1 ratio, then heaven must inject a strong force of about 15 into the mind, creating a 15 to 5 ratio, so that it can automatically lead the body. It aims to create a habit where the body becomes a person who dislikes what it wants to do. This is an undeniable movement to find a person for God to create unity. If one stands in a position to hate the evil side that serves the body and can resolve it, that person becomes aligned with heaven. 
Therefore, the teaching of religion is to deny what the body desires and, on the other hand, to devote oneself to receive God's strength. This has been the movement of religion up to now. Thus, God has sought to start from such an individual, moving to families, tribes, and nations, ultimately aiming for one nation, which was the nation of Israel and the Israelite people. In other words, they were the chosen people. Considering that the term "chosen people" or "chosen nation" exists in history, we cannot deny the existence of God. 
As God planned, individuals, families, tribes, and nations must become completely one, and He promised for a long time to send a representative who could unify the world. This is the concept of the Messiah. God intended to create a pattern of individual, family, nation, and world through the Israelite people, aiming to save the world. 
Jesus, who came as the prototype of the ideal (unity)
What you must understand here is that while there was certainly a purpose for the Israelite people to receive the Messiah and live well, God's providence was not to save just one nation but to save the world. This was the purpose of sending the Messiah. At that time, the desires of the Israelite people and the direction of God's providence needed to align, but they diverged. 
Thus, the individual Jesus, who came as the pattern of the unified world, was supposed to create a family pattern, a tribal pattern, a national pattern, and a global pattern, but he could not accomplish that. For example, the nation of Israel was like a field of wild olive trees that could be controlled at will. Jesus came as a true olive tree to cut down all the wild olive trees and to graft individuals and families into God's pattern. Then, would the nation of Israel and Judaism become true olive trees or wild olive trees? They would undoubtedly become true olive trees. If they had united around the nation and conducted global missions with the sovereignty of Judaism, the history of Christianity over the past 2,000 years would not have been necessary. 
However, before a world where body and mind are one, Jesus was sent to this earth as a basic unity pattern, but the Israelite people and Judaism crucified him. Because they became a Judaism and an Israelite nation opposing God's will, the nation and foundation that God had established for thousands of years turned to the side of Satan. Thus, the Israelite people became a nation without a country for 2,000 years, suffering under the hooves of many nations. 
In 1948, the nation of Israel gained independence. We must understand that the time has come for such independence, indicating that we have entered a global era where we can start anew. The time has come, and the Lord...
We must understand that the time for His return is drawing near. 
So, after Israel betrayed heaven throughout the historical process until now, 
do you think there were any foundations that God could use as a stepping stone, 
whether it be an individual foundation, a family foundation, a tribal foundation, 
or a national foundation? There were none. Christianity inherited this, and while 
the first Israel could not fulfill its purpose, the second Israel must take on the 
mission and fulfill it. However, Christianity has not been able to establish a 
foundation that unites the physical and spiritual realms, and we must recognize 
that it has been engaged in a movement seeking a nation that is spiritually focused 
while neglecting the physical realm.

In this perspective, is there a nation that God can claim, saying, "This is the 
nation I love"? There is none. The United States boasts of having nearly 200 million 
citizens, two-thirds of whom are Christians, but is this America the nation of God? 
No. Among the many nations in the democratic world, there is no nation that can 
claim, "This is my nation, my people, my land," no matter how small it may be. 
The Israelite people were at least prepared to welcome the Messiah, who would come 
with a nation and a church, but now Christianity is not preparing a nation and is 
only hoping spiritually. You must understand that this is a serious problem. There 
is no such nation in the world. There is no foundation where you can daily say to 
God, "Please accept this nation that my family is dedicating with sincerity!"

In the Old Testament era, people discussed matters with God using offerings, but 
has anyone in the New Testament era offered their entire being to discuss with God? 
No. Are the great pastors or bishops of America in that position? They are not. 
What you must understand is that the majority of pastors in America do not know 
whether God exists or not. I know there are many such pastors. They say, "Christianity 
is a religion for self-cultivation. What does it matter if God exists or not for 
self-cultivation?" And how many pastors are saying that communism is good? If God 
exists, would He want that? That means they are saying that whatever the body wants 
is acceptable. Such a thing cannot exist. When the WCC meeting was held in America 
recently, over 600 pastors gathered and shouted, "Support China! Support China!" 
You all know this.

We are living in serious times. Ideologies centered on materialism are dreaming of 
dominating the world, and you must recognize that they are advancing with a unified 
ideology from the top to the bottom. Is there a denomination among the American 
churches that can boast, "I have a land where I can serve God on behalf of America"? 
Is there a congregation that can claim, "My home, my entire livelihood, and my sons 
and daughters are all God's people"? When we think of a God without a foundation 
centered around a nation, the problem is significant.

Can the Lord, as Christians believe, return in the air and unify individuals, 
families, tribes, nations, and the world in such a pattern? No, it cannot. The 
destination that the returning Lord can achieve is not the air but the earth, this 
land, this world. Therefore, as Jesus became a man who formed a pattern, how can 
He establish a unified family with a completely united man and woman? This must 
be resolved for a unified nation and world to emerge.

Among today's Christians, is there anyone who thinks, "I will become a bride and 
create the family that the Lord desires"? They do not know the concrete content. 
They do not know where He will come from or how He will come. The Lord cannot 
come riding on clouds. He is coming to find the family that God desires. To find 
that family, it cannot stand alone. There must be a tribe that can support that 
family, a nation that can support that tribe, and a country that can support that 
nation. Without establishing a pattern that can be achieved centered on one nation, 
the current Christianity must understand that it cannot find the third Israel.

The thought of Christianity is the thought of service and sacrifice. 
Let us reflect again on the way for an individual to remain forever. To be a 
respected person in the world, one cannot be someone who elevates oneself. 
To be honored, one must sacrifice. If you have ten friends, the one who sacrifices 
for those ten friends for a long time becomes the central being in front of them. 
Not only them, but their relatives and friends will also want to unite with that 
person. Conversely, if there is someone who says to those ten friends, "You must 
do this for me. Do this for me," then those friends will distance themselves. 
They will become isolated. In the end, they will have nowhere to go. You must 
understand that this is the distinguishing point between good and evil in our 
society.

Let us look at a patriot of a nation. When you think of America, you highly respect 
President Lincoln or the recently deceased President Kennedy. Why do you respect 
them? They are both presidents, but you respect them because they sacrificed their 
lives for America. If there is a president among them who died miserably for 
America, the more miserable the sacrifice, the higher he will hold the position of 
a patriot and president in America.

If we were to choose the most devoted president among five presidents, the ones who 
did not die would not even be considered. The more one loves the nation with their 
life, the greater they are, especially if they were sacrificed miserably. The more 
miserable it is, the more it may be miserable at one time, but as history passes, 
the scope of the environment will gradually expand around them.

The death of Jesus was the same. For whom did Jesus sacrifice? For the entire 
humanity, for the nations of the world. He loved humanity more than anyone else, 
loved God more than anyone else, and even loved His enemies, praying for them and 
miserably passing away. No one could have known that the nameless Jesus, who was 
once labeled a national traitor, would establish a global Christian cultural realm.

Here we can present a principle. Those who sacrifice for a great stage, for a 
public great work, do not perish. We can know that they do not perish. Such people 
are historical figures.

So, is it bad to sacrifice for others? The question is what the result will be after 
the sacrifice. People naturally want to serve that person. They want to be governed 
by someone who gives to them until the end.

In light of this, if God exists, and if God has a strategy to fight against the 
world of evil, we can discover what that strategy is. Evil is the opposite. It 
sacrifices others for its own benefit. If this happens personally, it faces 
opposition from individuals, and if it goes out like this on a family or national 
level, it will inevitably be condemned by history as a dictator. This must be 
understood clearly.

The strategy of evil is to sacrifice others to rise, while God's strategy is to 
sacrifice oneself to save others. Therefore, those who claimed goodness throughout 
the historical process were not welcomed in their time and were sacrificed, but 
those who loved their country and the world while sacrificing their bodies will have 
their names revealed as history passes. This is a fact that cannot be denied.

Therefore, what is the thought of Christianity? It is the thought of service and 
sacrifice. If Christianity becomes a religion that only serves its own denomination, 
it will perish. If any Christian denomination in America focuses all its activities 
on saving America and is prepared to make any sacrifice to achieve that purpose, 
heaven will cooperate. If Christianity can become a nation that sacrifices American 
citizens to save the world, it can be seen as a Christianity that can dominate the 
world.

The reason God blesses America 
When we consider whether God loves America or the world, we must understand that 
God should love the world more than America. Therefore, when it is time to pay the 
price of sacrifice to save the world, America must be put forward.

American citizens! Do you believe there is a traditional ideological legacy in 
America that can be said to be like this? Among the current youth, it may be hard 
to find. The people who pioneered America, as you know, were the Puritans. They 
were people who came to this new continent, America, because the state blocked 
their way to love God freely. At that time, a small number of Americans risked 
their lives to fight against the local Indians, clinging to God. I know that the 
ideology of that struggle, which revered God, became the founding ideology of America. 
That is why they built churches first, then schools, and only then did they build 
their homes.

Because they stood in such a position, God brought them out from opposing 
environments and protected them, allowing them to establish a global nation within 
less than 200 years. What do you think God blessed them for? You should not think 
that He blessed them to make those living in America prosperous. It should be seen 
that God blessed them to make them a representative nation to save the world.

However, do the American people have a unified ideology saying, "Now let us unite to 
save the world"? They do not. However, the communist world, which is America's enemy, 
is emerging with the confidence that it can dominate the world and swallow America 
without any problem. You must know that the struggle between black and white in 
your country is becoming increasingly intense. The communists are expanding their 
base centered around the blacks who are opposed by whites.

These days, the peoples of Asia are all afraid of China. Do you think there is a 
country in Asia that can stop the expansion of the communist world and defend God's 
side? Who do you think will do that for the Asian countries? America has begun to 
provide aid to Asia. This is a historical event that has not occurred in the 
historical era. If you have started doing the right thing, you must see it through 
to the end. If it is a good thing, it is an extremely good thing. To sacrifice for 
others and to help others is something that heaven can always bless and praise. 
However, this has been turning back after 20 years. While trying to find itself, 
America must not forget that it has lost the world.

What American citizens must remember is that cutting back on foreign aid, such as 
aid to Asia, is not God's will. You see, the president who started cutting back on 
foreign aid was President Kennedy. At that time, the UN Secretary-General was 
Dag Hammarskjöld. We think that there must have been some unknown motivation behind 
why those people suffered such disasters.

In 1965, I met President Eisenhower. At that time, I pointed out that while he may 
think that the truce he made during the Korean War was a good thing, it was a 
historical error. I asked him if he believed in communism, saying that communists 
are people whose words and actions differ. You must understand that their actions 
and words are different. After the truce agreement, we are now seeing North Korea 
arming its citizens with all its might. Will you deny this fact?

I know that February 21 is the day of the meeting between Mao Zedong and 
President Nixon. Mao Zedong has nothing to lose whether he attacks President Nixon 
or not. American citizens must understand this. The communists can say "we are 
close, we are close" to America and then just turn around. They are a dictatorship 
that can retreat just as easily as they advance.

However, American citizens cannot do that. If the entire America says it is good 
and all the citizens go out, if they retreat from here, do you think all American 
citizens will retreat? You must understand that half will split apart. I am now 
thinking about what will happen to America at that time. From this perspective, I 
see the history of America’s 40th president, up to the year 210, as a history 
protected by God.

You see, I know that 1976 is the 200th anniversary of the founding of America. 
From Abraham to Jesus, there are 42 generations. The history of 40 generations has 
been centered on God's will. Although there are 42 generations in total, we count 
the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob as one God, which is 
why it becomes 40 generations.

To save the world, we must transcend the nation. 
I believe that such a history of indemnity centered on America will take place at 
the end of this age. If we fail to take responsibility during this period, I believe 
that America will not continue to be a nation protected by God. I think this way. 
In the latter half of the 20th century, if America, which bore the responsibility of 
being a leading nation in the world, does not boast, even if the nation of America 
disappears, if the American people have an ideology that they can boast of, then 
even in the 30th and 40th centuries, that ideology must be maintained, and if they 
have such an ideology, the American people can become a people who can dominate the 
world.

From this perspective, the question will be what mission our Unification Church is 
trying to undertake. The Unification Church is preparing a global movement to welcome 
the Lord who is coming, with the bride, to establish the hopeful kingdom that God 
desires on this earth.

To do this, the Unification Church must eliminate the idea of working for itself. 
God's strategy requires individuals, families, tribes, and nations that can sacrifice 
for the world, and our mission is to organize such individuals, families, and tribes 
to create the foundation of the nation that God desires.

With the principle of such unity, who will lead as a unified individual, bride, 
family, tribe, and nation centered on the coming Messiah? Will it be the unbelievers 
or the believers? Will it be those with religion or those without? It must be those 
who believe in Christianity and religious people who must come together to do this 
work. This is the movement that must be done in the world now.

Therefore, do not unite centered on your denomination or my denomination.
position due to the bloodline of Satan. This is the fundamental issue that we must understand.

The providence of God is to restore humanity, and this restoration cannot happen without addressing the bloodline issue. The blood of Satan has infiltrated our very beings, and it is this blood that must be purged for us to return to God. Therefore, God has always been engaged in a struggle to establish His will on earth.

If Adam and Eve had not fallen and had remained in the position that God desired, we would have seen a different outcome. I mentioned on the first night that God placed humanity in the position of His most beloved sons and daughters. Humans have a desire not only for the position of sons and daughters but also to be in the same position as God. If Adam and Eve had fulfilled their role, God would have entered into them, and they would have become one with Him.

In 1 Corinthians 3:16, it states that our bodies are temples of God. Even fallen humanity can become a temple of God when they reach the position of salvation, and this is even more true for Adam and Eve before the Fall. If that had been the case, God would have entered into their bodies, becoming their inner God, while Adam and Eve would have manifested the outer body of God. This unity would have allowed them to grow in love and establish a family that was not just theirs but also God's family. In other words, God would have become the Father of humanity, and humanity would have been born with God's bloodline.

If this had happened, there would have been no internal struggle within individuals. There would have been no basis for evil to invade our bodies. If individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world had reached this state, we would have seen the realization of the Kingdom of Heaven on earth, and when transitioning to the heavenly realm, all of humanity would have ascended together.

In Romans 8, it says, "We cry out, 'Abba, Father,' and wait for our adoption." Even if humanity is saved, we can only be adopted as children. This indicates a difference in bloodline. So, why are we in this position? It is because we have formed a blood relationship with Satan. Because we received the corrupted bloodline of Satan, even if we are saved, we can only be adopted as children.

Now, let us examine the relationship between God and Satan. Satan is the enemy who has destroyed God's beloved family. God cannot forgive Satan. The day God forgives Satan will be the day the universe is turned upside down, and everything will be destroyed. Individuals who inherit the blood of Satan establish families, tribes, and nations, spreading the bloodline, which naturally leads to Satan becoming the king of all humanity. Originally, humanity was meant to be the children of the rightful owner, but due to the bloodline of Satan, we have become slaves.
It has become that we have become sons. Satan intercepted what God was trying to do by raising Adam and Eve to create God's family in the future. Therefore, we must clearly understand that Satan is the enemy of God and the enemy who has taken away the original ideal of humanity. 

Because of this, we have lost the way to receive God's lineage and become God's sons and daughters. We must recognize that humanity has been longing for that path while going through a history of groaning until now. 

Ultimately, since we have become the sons and daughters of Satan, we have been embraced in Satan's bosom and have become the servants of servants before God. Therefore, we must draw these servants of servants out of Satan and create people like God's servants, placing those who dedicate themselves to God's will among them in the position of God's adopted children, gradually raising them up.

Thus, God has been working since the Old Testament era to raise humans from the position of servants of servants to the position of adopted children. This is to establish the right of adoption. That right of adoption is the nation of Israel. In other words, the nation of Israel is the chosen servants and adopted children on God's side, selected from the world of Satan. This is like a field of wild olive trees that God can manage as He pleases.

In this way, God has raised the nation of Israel from the position of servants of servants to that of servants and adopted children, preparing the nation of Israel until the coming of the son. Based on that foundation, He intended to send the Messiah as the true olive tree, to graft the entire nation of Israel, like a field of wild olive trees, to create a nation of rightful sovereignty that God could govern. This has been the overview of God's providential history up to now.

Since we can only be adopted children, we cannot become God's sons and daughters without the direct lineage son coming to graft us. God promised through the prophets to send the Messiah to the nation of Israel and sent Jesus after 2,000 years, but the nation of Israel and the church should have united and become one with Jesus completely, but because they could not, Jesus had to die. If they had become one, Jesus would have become the high priest of Judaism and the king of the Jewish nation.

The issue here is that Jesus was single. Shouldn't he be single to become a priest and single to become a king? That cannot be. If Jesus had married, what would have happened? A family centered around Jesus would have emerged. Furthermore, Jesus could have fulfilled the position of true parents that Adam and Eve were supposed to achieve without falling.

If Christians came here, they would be surprised, saying, "Oh! Could Jesus do that?" This person standing here also attended a Presbyterian church and believed in Jesus. Upon delving into the content, I realized that this is how it turned out. I have faced much opposition for speaking such things. However, it is undeniable that it is the truth. No matter how much I go to the spiritual world and check, there is no other way, and because I know this is the truth, I have set out on this path, prepared to face death and pioneering the path of persecution.

Wouldn't Jesus, being a man, have wanted to welcome a bride and have children? Wouldn't he have wanted to hear the word "father" on this earth? Of course, he would have wanted to hear it. He would have wanted to hear people calling him father. He would have also wanted to hear the word "grandfather." If Jesus had become a priest and the king of Israel, a royal lineage that God could govern would have emerged. If that had happened, today there would have been direct descendants of Jesus left in this world.

Would God love the direct descendants of Jesus more than the nation of Israel, or less? Who would He love more? If that had happened, centered around Jesus, Christians would have formed a kingdom of royal authority, a nation of rightful sovereignty, spreading out into the world. This is something that can be understood even from a common-sense perspective. Wouldn't you think the same if you stood in the same position as Jesus as a man? Wouldn't you want that?

One God and One World Religion
Good evening, ladies and gentlemen. I sincerely thank you for attending this event. Philadelphia is a place that can be commemorated as the first in American history, and I believe it is a place we can be proud of in the historical process. I consider it an infinite honor to have a gathering with you in such a place.

As you can see, I am an Eastern person. When you think of 'Korea,' I believe you cannot forget the impressions of the Korean War. It is not easy to come from Korea to meet you here in America. I have hoped for about 20 years to meet you in such an official setting, and I first want to express my gratitude to God for this meeting and to you as well.

This evening, I would like to speak briefly on the topic of "One God and One World Religion."

Does God Exist?
When we look at the current world situation and think about who will take responsibility for this world, it becomes increasingly clear that this is a serious issue. February 8, 1972 (Tuesday), Sheraton Hotel (Philadelphia, USA).

If God exists, that God will guide this world correctly. It is our urgent desire that God must guide this world.

However, there are many people on this planet who do not even know whether God exists or not. If they knew that God existed, even if they were told not to follow Him, individuals, countless nations, and the entire world would have no choice but to follow where He goes and where He intends. Therefore, whether He exists or not is the issue. Only if He exists will there be a religion that seeks His will and follows the direction to fulfill that will. If God does not exist, then talk of world religions or anything else is unnecessary for us. Since the existence of God is the issue, let us briefly discuss this matter.

The Requirements of Existence and Action
We know that this world is an existing world. On a large scale, the solar system exists, and on a small scale, atoms exist. Generally, we understand that in order to exist, there must be power. It is because of power that existence is possible. Without power, existence cannot occur. However, the question is whether power comes first or existence comes first. Existence is due to power. For that power to exist, action must take place. Without action, existence cannot continue. Power must act to exist. If there is no action, power cannot exist.

In action, one cannot act alone. We can conclude that there must be a subject and an object. For example, if the President of the United States were to speak or sing alone in joy, everyone would say that he is not a normal person. However, if he smiles while looking at a small clock or something, it would be strange to think of him as odd.

Let us assume there is an absolute God. No matter how high that God is, He cannot be joyful alone. If that absolute being were to be happy and laugh alone, we could not say that this God is a normal God. However, if that absolute God were to express admiration and joy in relation to a small counterpart, then it would be the one who says He is crazy who is actually crazy.

Thus, we can realize how precious the object is; without an object, all actions are worthless. Therefore, when there is no counterpart, action is a futile action. Joy and all such feelings are meaningless without an object. This is an undeniable fact.

If there is an absolute subject and a person who can be that subject's counterpart, action will inevitably occur. However, in action, there is no action that results in loss. In the relationship between the subject and the object, if the purposes of the subject and the object diverge, action will not occur. Action occurs only when something is discovered that can be beneficial to both the subject and the object.

I do not know the name of the bustling area in Philadelphia. If there is a Market Street, many people will pass through it. When you go out to Market Street, if someone says, "I am going out to Market Street to incur a loss," everyone would consider that person insane. There would be no one like that. When one goes out, they must be hoping for something that can be beneficial to them. They absolutely do not want to engage in actions that would result in loss. They must not and cannot do so.

From this perspective, the reason this vast universe could come into being is that it pursued the value of a purpose that could yield more benefits through action, and thus it could develop into something greater. If actions were taken that led to diminishment, this universe could cease to exist at some point. Therefore, you cannot deny the notion that there must be a subject and an object in action. Thus, we can conclude that there must necessarily be a subject and an object in action.

God's Ultimate Counterpart is Humanity
Now, let us return to the question of whether there is an absolute God or not. God cannot be alone; He must take a counterpart. So what will He take as a counterpart in this universe? Plants? Animals? Animals are slightly better than plants. If we ask what the absolute and supreme God would take as a counterpart among all creation, even kindergarten children would say it is humanity.

Humans are the masterpieces among all created beings in this universe. They are such masterpieces that they are immeasurably great and beautiful. If the absolute God exists and created humans, could He make them in such a way that they would not know what He thinks, sees, or feels?

Let us liken God to an artist. An artist thinks in their heart and conceives in their mind to create the best work. When the one and only masterpiece is created, it becomes an unparalleled work, and the artist feels infinite joy. If that work turns out to be even more beautiful than they envisioned, no one would say, "It turned out differently than I thought, so I will break it!" Rather, they would treasure it as the greatest treasure of their life and want to show it off, which is an undeniable sentiment of an artist. If we think this way, how much more would the absolute God, who created humanity, want to create humans as the finest masterpieces?

Among the audience here, is there anyone who would not want to make God their own if He exists? Raise your hand. Whether man or woman, whether talented or not, whether healthy or disabled, everyone wants to make the best their own. This is a desire that everyone possesses. The desire for this is an action that occurs in the relationship between the subject and the object. If one thinks this way, it is impossible to act without the possibility of achieving the purpose.

Therefore, if there is an absolute God who created humans, the purposes of that God and the purposes of humanity must not diverge. A point of convergence must be established where both can completely unite, so that God can say, "Ah! I have fulfilled My will. Ah! It is a masterpiece!" and only then can we truly engage with it.

The Existence of God is Evident through the Conscience of Humanity
God desires for humanity, and humanity must look up to God. Because humanity cannot exist without God, this directionality is something God has permitted, and we must understand that this is the action of conscience. In this regard, it is not a loss for God to meet humanity, nor is it a loss for humanity to meet God. They must meet because it is good for both.

Now we can conclude that our conscience has always desired to dominate the world and to become the highest being since the inception of humanity. Given that there is a directional aspect to this conscience, we can conclude that action requires a counterpart, and action without a counterpart cannot exist. Therefore, for our conscience to act, there must be something subjective to that conscience. Thus, conscience itself does not engage in actions that result in loss. Actions without a subject or without a counterpart violate principles, leading us to conclude that God absolutely exists.

Among the audience here, there may be someone who is unsure whether God exists. So let us now think about whether God truly exists or not, centered around ourselves.

The Existence of God through the Mystery of the Human Body
The most important part of our body is the head. Look closely at your eyes. They are so wonderfully made. Now, why are our eyes shaped this way? They came to be because our father existed, our grandmother existed, and so on, back to the first ancestors of humanity who had such eyes.

When our ancestral grandparents were born, did they know whether the Earth existed or whether celestial bodies existed? This eye, upon being born on Earth, not only knew about the ground but also prepared for the existence of the solar system. Did this eye know the Earth and the sun by itself?

Also, look. The eyes blink. When the sun shines on the ground, it creates radiant heat, causing moisture to evaporate. If the moisture in your eyes evaporates due to this heat, it would be a big problem. It must not evaporate. Because it would be a big problem, the eyelids blink to prevent evaporation and to keep them moist. Did the eyes know this by themselves? Look at the eyebrows. The eyebrows knew there would be dust before coming to the ground. They were made to prevent dust from entering the eyes. How did they know this? Did they say, "There is dust, so I will grow like this?" The eyebrows already knew that humans would stand and walk. They knew there would be sweat. Because the eyes are recessed, if sweat were to flow in, it would enter like a drain, so they established a defense line to prevent that. Did the eyebrows know this by themselves? Look at the nose. What if the nose were attached upside down? (Laughter) It knew it should not be upside down, so it is attached this way. The nose also knew there would be dust in the air.

Why is everything designed this way? Have you ever thought about it? Why is the mouth shaped like this? It is designed to prevent anything from entering. The eyes are fully exposed, and the mouth is fully exposed. Look at the ears. They are designed to hear all sounds from others. If one were to hear without any adjustment, it would be a big problem, so they are structured to filter sounds through the mountains and valleys. Did they know all this before they were born?

Even if a university professor or a famous scholar were here, would anyone say, "I came out not knowing all this. I wanted to come out like this?" It is undeniable that they knew everything before they were born. They knew. But did the person born know this? Did humanity come out knowing all this? This body is like a corporation of hundreds or thousands of medical doctors. It knows everything. It has been designed to align with biological and astronomical knowledge. However, because Cain killed Abel to receive God's love, the providential work...
It has been extended.

Does God Exist?

As you look at the current world situation, you know that the question of where the world is headed in the future is a serious issue. Even if God exists, nothing can be accomplished by God alone. If God exists, He must need humanity more than anything else in the universe. If God created this world, we can view Him as the author and this world as His work.

Today, people living on this earth know that the universe exists. It is commonly said that existence comes from power. Without power, there can be no existence. When we think about this power, there must be an action that precedes it. Without continuous action, power ceases.

The Principle of Action

To take action, one cannot act alone. There must be a prerequisite for action, which is the relationship between subject and object. Thus, we can conclude that for power to exist, action must occur, and for action to happen, there must be both a subject and an object.

In the action between a subject and an object, neither side will act if one is at a disadvantage. Therefore, the fact that action begins means that there are conditions under which the purpose of the subject and the purpose of the object can both be positively fulfilled. When there are no conditions for a positive outcome, action will not occur. In other words, action does not happen when it leads to a loss.

You have come here this evening. I believe that none of you came here to incur a loss. It is certain that you came seeking something that could bring you a gain. If coming here would result in a loss, you would not continue to act.

In Baltimore, there is a bustling downtown area. Many people are coming and going there. Among those who go out onto the street, there is not a single person who would say, 'I am going out today to incur a loss.' Everyone is moving to find something that can be beneficial, something that can contribute positively. If there is no benefit, that movement will not continue. It will come to a halt. In any business, both parties must discover a purpose that can be beneficial for themselves in order to act.

If I were to make gestures with no one around, people would say I am crazy. However, if I were to do this to catch something, I would not be considered insane. Let’s say there is a world-famous figure in this country. If that person were to laugh and dance alone in a room, everyone would call him crazy. But if he were to hold a cup, shout, sing, and dance, then he would not be considered insane.

From this perspective, let’s assume there is an absolute being at the center of this universe, God. If God were to laugh and chatter alone without anything, He would be considered an odd God. However, if He speaks or laughs based on something small, we understand that He is a God in a normal position. Here, we can see that for all actions and powers to continue, there must be a relationship between subject and object, and they must be based on principles that can mutually benefit each other.

If you conduct a chemical experiment centered on some element, no matter how much a person tries to combine elements through their own power, they cannot do so alone. However, when two elements interact as subjects and objects, and if conditions arise that allow them to combine and become more than they were before, then action occurs.

The same applies to men and women in this world. When a man and a woman come together, if it results in even a slight disadvantage for either, no matter how much they try to unite, they will not. However, when they see the possibility of being better than they are now or are directed towards a better place, they will act and come together. When that union holds infinite value, they will become one in a position that can never be separated.

Therefore, to exist, there must be power, and for power to exist, action must occur, and for action to happen, there must be a subject and an object. Ultimately, we must understand that existence continues only where the subject and object can grow larger. It is through such actions that small things can grow and form the vast universe. They can become relative and thus achieve this. If actions were to occur that lead to diminishment, the value of the elements would be destroyed. There can be no unity where conflicting actions exist. Only where there is mutual reinforcement and the power to grow further can there be unity.

From this perspective, the philosophy of dialectics that communists emphasize, which has become a global issue today, is a significant problem. Therefore, there is no existence without a purpose, and there is no development where a better purpose is not pursued. When it comes to humanity, we are beings of consequence. We exist because of some cause.

The Existence of God Through the Action of Conscience

We humans have the action of conscience. The action of conscience urges us to go towards goodness. This action of conscience cannot be denied by anyone. It operates continuously, managing us day and night. Even if you suddenly wake up at night and try to do something bad, your conscience will say, 'Hey!' and restrain you.

When we consider the continuous management and action of our conscience, we previously mentioned that action does not occur without the establishment of a subject-object relationship. We said that action does not happen when it anticipates a negative outcome. We said that action occurs because a value can be established that is better. Therefore, when we look at the action of conscience, it is unquestionable that there must be some relationship between the conscience as a result or as a subject.

We humans are not the subject. Therefore, there must be something that is the subject. Whether in the past, now, or thousands of years from now, there is no revolution or development in the action of conscience. Because that subject is absolute, it cannot change as long as that subject does not change.

When we see that there is a subject that can act upon our conscience, the question is, what is that subject? We cannot say that this subject does not exist. Whether we call that subject God or something else, every nation has its own name for it. Regardless of the name, the existence of that subject is a fact. We can call that subject God.

If we quietly observe our human body, it is a palace of mystery. When we trace back to our human ancestors, we arrive at the very first ancestor. If we consider that ancestor to be Adam, let’s think about that one grandfather Adam. He was born on the earth. As a person born on the earth, do you think he thought, 'When I am born on the earth, I need to have eyes shaped this way to see the sun in the sky'? No, when he was born, his eyes were prepared not only to see the earth but also to see the sunlight in the sky.

Your eyes are blinking. This is because it is known that vapor evaporates from the earth due to radiant heat, and it is necessary to prevent that evaporation, so they blink. Now, would you blink without knowing this fact? Try not blinking for 30 minutes and see what happens. It would be a disaster.

Now look at your eyelashes. Why are they attached here? Do you think they just happened to be there without knowing that there is dust in the air? They are already there because they know there is dust in the air. Consider what would happen if those eyelashes were not there. Sweat would definitely accumulate here, and that would be a big problem. Therefore, it is clear that they were designed with the knowledge that a person would stand and walk.

Next, look at your eyes. They are not sunken in; they are slightly protruding. Look at your nose. Why is it shaped this way? What if it were inverted? (Laughter) Everyone, the nose is shaped like this for a reason. The upper part is narrow, and as it goes down, it widens to prevent anything from entering the mouth. There is no one without a nose. Is there anyone with a nose that is shaped differently? (Laughter) It has been designed to keep things as far away as possible. And the mouth is not recessed; it is well designed.

When we observe these things, can we think that they happened by chance or that they were made arbitrarily? Even the nose and eyes were designed with the knowledge that there is dust in the air. The ears also have hair because they know there is dust in the air. The human ear is structured to hear sounds directly because it knows how to receive sound from high and low mountains.

Now, look at your hands. They are all designed to function in front of you. There are many people in the world who claim that these were made to adapt arbitrarily. **The Path of Victory**

Neither Buddha, Confucius, nor Muhammad had such a background. Only by doing so can one escape from the world of Satan. Only then can one finally receive God's love. It is essential to believe in places where one cannot believe and to come out from places where one cannot emerge in order to receive God's love.

Looking at the time of Noah, God commanded Noah to do what seemed impossible. He did not tell him to build the ark by the riverside but rather on the mountaintop. Look at Abraham. Abraham was living a comfortable life with love in his family. Without any promise of future blessings, he became part of a band of gypsies crossing borders.

Regardless of the difficulties, with a heart that does not distrust God but believes absolutely, even if he falls into hardship, overcoming it and hoping to stand closer to heaven, that is why God could not help but bless Abraham's descendants to be as numerous as the sand of the sea and the stars in the sky.

The same goes for Jacob. He left home without caring about life and death after receiving blessings.

Look at Moses. Moses believed more than anyone that God loved the chosen people of Israel, and he left the palace of Pharaoh for their sake. You see, John the Baptist is the same. John the Baptist left his home and spent 30 years in the wilderness, eating locusts and wild honey, overcoming all hardships to fulfill God's will.

When we look at all these ancestors of faith that appeared in the history of the Israelite nation, we see that they believed in places where they could not believe and overcame difficulties that could not be overcome through struggle, thus becoming people who could receive God's love. Today, rather than discussing the spiritual world, the title of my message is "One God and One World Religion," delivered on February 28, 1972, at the Ambassador Hotel in Los Angeles, USA. * This message was given during a public lecture tour in seven major cities in the United States.

God, who needs a subject
Looking at the current world situation, the question of where humanity will go in the future is a significant issue that cannot be overlooked by the global community. If there is an absolute and omnipotent God, it is certain that He will guide this world correctly. I believe that many people who are concerned about world issues think inwardly about how wonderful it would be if God exists. 

When we consider the issue of one God and one world religion, it is clear that nothing can exist without humanity. From individuals to families, nations, and the world, such concepts cannot be established without all of humanity. Therefore, if God exists, He must need humanity and cannot help but seek to fulfill His providential purpose through humanity. To realize God's providence, it is essential to go through a religious form. For this reason, I believe that God cannot help but desire a world religion.

So, what is the problem here? People are aware of their existence, but many do not have a clear understanding of whether God exists or not among the global population today. 

Let us briefly discuss whether God actually exists. Many people know that the universe exists. We humans also exist. To exist, certain conditions must be met, and actions are necessary for continued existence. Without action, existence cannot be sustained. Action does not occur in isolation; it requires both a subject and an object. We know that where there is no relationship between the subject and the object, we cannot observe any phenomena of action. Continuous action can only occur where there is both a subject and an object.

If I stand here with nothing and wave my hands, you would laugh and think I am strange. However, if there is even a small object, something barely visible, and I see it moving up and down, you would consider me a normal person. In America, if the President were to laugh and dance alone in an empty room, everyone watching would think he is crazy. But if he were to hold a small object, like a glass, and enjoy it while laughing and dancing, then he would be considered a normal president. We must recognize how precious relative existence and objects are.

If there is an absolute being, God, who is the center of the universe, then it follows that this absolute being also needs an object. If we consider God as the center, we should think about what kind of object He would take from this created world. It would not be plants. It would not be animals either. Of course, animals are somewhat better than plants. Since God is absolute, He must stand in a position to relate to the highest object. Among all created beings, what is the highest existence? Even a kindergarten student would know this. Therefore, we cannot deny that among all created beings, humans are the greatest masterpiece.

The highest purpose desired by God and humanity
If there is such an absolute God who created the created world and humanity, there must be some connection through which God and humanity can relate. If God created humanity, then the purpose of His creation and the purpose of the created beings must not be separate; otherwise, they cannot establish a relationship. If we cannot find a point of unity centered around one purpose, it goes without saying that humanity and God cannot achieve a common joy. From this perspective, we can conclude that the highest purpose desired by the supreme being is also the point of human desire. Therefore, there must be some action that allows us to reach that purpose.

For this reason, our hearts desire the highest purpose. Human desire is driven by the pursuit of the highest purpose. If there is a great person in the world, you want to establish a relationship with that person. It is not just about meeting them; it is the desire of humanity to establish a loving relationship with them.

Among you who are present, if God exists, there would be no one who does not want to make God their own. Regardless of gender, regardless of whether one is talented or not, regardless of whether one is disabled or not, it is impossible not to desire this. If it were possible, everyone would wish for it. Therefore, in the pursuit of the highest, people are equal.

Even if one claims to have conquered God, people are not satisfied with that. If there is a unique love hidden within God, the desire to conquer that love also arises. The ultimate destination of human desire is not just to conquer God, but to conquer God's love as well. When one conquers God's love, all that belongs to God becomes theirs.

The principle of action
As mentioned earlier, action occurs in the relationship between a subject and an object. It is undeniable that for action to continue, there must be both a subject and an object. The action of our conscience is rushing toward a vast and great goal.

So, how great is the conscience? Viewed narrowly, it is very small; viewed broadly, it is wider than the entire universe. Your desire wants to be greater than God. This desire has been acting and moving along with the direction of history without any change since humanity came into existence.

In action, there is no law that operates for mutual loss. When you came here tonight, you did not come to say, "Oh, Mr. Moon has come to Los Angeles; I want to see what kind of man he is," with the intention of losing something. If someone were to say, "I am going out today to incur a loss," that person would be considered insane. 

When there is a loss in action, it cannot continue. This is also true in love between a man and a woman. If someone intends to incur a loss in dealing with their partner, that person is not human. For a man and a woman to unite, they must have a standard that allows them to remain united forever; otherwise, they will fail. If the principle of diminishing exists in action, this vast universe would not have formed. Therefore, because there is something that allows two entities to act together and benefit each other, the universe can unite toward a great purpose.

When conducting a chemistry experiment, even if the experimenter tries to force the elements to react, they will not react. However, when two entities appear that can benefit each other, they will react even if told not to.

The principle of action revolves around the relationship between the subject and the object, and we can conclude that without a purposeful content that allows both entities to gain, action will not occur. Those who study natural sciences or believe in dialectics may find this statement strange, but I believe it is worth reconsidering.

When we see that humans have a conscience, we cannot deny the existence of God. The existence of conscience is absolutely undeniable. There is not a single person who lacks conscience. If someone were to say, "You have no conscience," everyone would get angry. Therefore, conscience exists in everyone.

You are well aware that this conscience pursues the highest authority, the highest position, and the highest value. If there is a supreme God and His love, then the question arises whether there can still be a conscience after conquering that love. If one conquers that, everything becomes theirs. Everything is contained within that.

From this perspective, action does not occur in a way that incurs loss in the relationship between the subject and the object. In this regard, our conscience action may seem to operate in a way that is not believed or that incurs loss, but that is not the case. God is such a being that if we can meet Him, we can act to meet Him at the highest position. If both God and humanity incur losses, that action will cease. However, if at any time there is a value that can be beneficial, you must understand that our conscience cannot help but act through history and through our lives.

When we observe this conscience action, for action to occur, there must be no loss. Also, when viewed from the perspective of the relationship between the subject and the object, as long as we cannot deny this conscience action, we are always a result-oriented existence rather than a subjective existence.

When we consider the pursuit of a more valuable content that can benefit the relationship between the subject and the object, it is undeniable that there must be a subject. From this perspective, I have suggested that God exists. Some may still think, "I am not sure!"

The existence of God through the mystery of the human body
Now, let us take an example centered around the human body, which is closest to us. Among our bodies, the most precious part is the head, more than the hands. Interestingly, it is structured in three stages and has seven openings. The ears connect to all sides. In the Bible, the number seven is considered a number of completion. In this sense, it makes sense that humans have seven openings.

When you wake up in the morning, you look in the mirror. You ask yourself how you look. The eyes are the most precious part of humanity. Among our facial features, the eyes symbolize God. The nose symbolizes Adam and Eve, representing humanity. The mouth, being the means through which we consume food and interact with the world, symbolizes all things. I am not asking you to believe this absolutely; I just want you to consider it.

What causes the universe to operate? In other words, what causes the head to function? It is because of the eyes. The eyes are the reason for movement; without them, there is no need. Therefore, the universe operates centered around God.

What is at the forefront of the human face? It is the nose. What stands at the forefront of the universe? It is humanity. The nose is formed by two nostrils coming together as one. If men and women do not completely unite, it becomes as stuffy as a blocked nostril. (Laughter) Through the mouth, we consume all things. Due to time constraints, I will move on.

If you closely observe your eyes and ask where they came from, you would answer, "They came from my mother and father." If someone were to say, "Your mother and father did not have eyes," that would be a big problem. Therefore, it is certain that both your parents had eyes, and your grandparents had eyes as well. If we trace back to the fundamental origin of those eyes, we arrive at the first human ancestors.

When the first human ancestors were born, eyes were created. They were born with eyes not to see the ground but to see the light. Before being born, they already knew that the sun existed. The question arises: Did the eyes themselves know this? They were born with an astronomical perspective.

Another interesting point is that your eyes blink. When moisture in your eyes evaporates due to sunlight, it is crucial to blink to protect the eyes from drying out. The eyelids already knew this and were born prepared to blink. Did the eyelids know that there was moisture in the air?

Additionally, there are large eyebrows above the eyes. Why are they dark? Think about it. Why were eyebrows designed to be dark? Humans walk upright, and if sweat drips down into the precious eyes, it would be a disaster; thus, a defensive line was established. Without eyebrows, water would surely collect in deep valleys, but they block that from happening. 

Do you know why the nose is shaped this way? What if the nose were inverted? (Laughter) The nose must be shaped this way. Have you considered whether the lower part is wider than the upper part? The lower part must be wider to allow the sweat to flow sideways rather than into the mouth. 

Look at the mouth. When sweat drips down, it also flows sideways. Everything is born knowing how to function perfectly, to the extent that even scientists cannot fully comprehend it.

When we look at the entire body, it is the palace of the mysteries of the universe. Here, there are countless research materials for medical doctors. This did not come about by chance. We cannot deny the conclusion that we began to exist on a foundation where everything was prepared. Now, when you were born...
I didn't know that. Did you know when you were born, or did you not know? You were born not knowing. No one could know that. Therefore, while we may not know that itself, we cannot deny that a resultant existence was born through someone who knows.

Who is the one who knows this completely? Whether it be God or some absolute being, you can attach any name to it. So let’s say there seems to be a God, or we can say there is one and move on.

The relationship between God and humans
God exists. The question is, what relationship does that God have with us humans? It would be a big problem if we could see the one God with our own eyes. This is not about the ideological conflict between the U.S. and the Soviet Union. A global war to seize God will continue forever. If you believe that God exists, wouldn’t you want to occupy that God? You would want to, right? If God were visible, a major incident would occur. Therefore, you must understand that the God who knows this must be an invisible God. (laughter)

If you occupied a visible God, the world would know and would try to seize it all; where would you hide it? There would be no place to hide. That is why those who want to occupy God would think, “Ah, it would be nice if God were invisible.” They would want to hide the invisible God in a place only they know, where others do not. Just as we humans can think like this, God must have also thought about it.

Then the question is, where is the place that only I know and others do not? That place is our conscience. If you have occupied God, you would want to hide Him in your conscience, a place where others cannot see, so that only you can know Him. Therefore, when you think, “I alone want to know,” your heart must be infinitely large. Our hearts can be infinitely large.

We have learned that God is a God of love. We also understand that humans are willing to give up everything for the highest love. Then whom does God love? Does He love Himself? No. God loves people because He is relative. And when we humans love God, we want to love Him from a position close to Him, because God is a relative subject. No matter how absolute God is, He wants to love alongside humans. We must understand what kind of place that loving relationship would be.

Would you prefer to be God's son-in-law, daughter-in-law, adopted son, or adopted daughter? Humans will strive for something higher if it exists. Ultimately, if there is a position of sons and daughters, it leads to the conclusion that everyone cannot help but desire to be in the position of God's sons and daughters. Among those who have come here, is there anyone who confidently says, “Ah, I am a son of God, I am a daughter of God”? Is there anyone who has become that? People strive to become that, but no one has actually stood in that position. The question is why they only strive to become it and cannot stand in that position.

Even if they claim to stand in that position, humans are not satisfied with it. In hoping for God, since God is absolute and has the power of creation, humans want to possess that creative power as well.

Looking at the relationship of wealth, the father is above, and the son is below. That is, it is a hierarchical relationship. When the son says, “I want to rise to my father’s position,” and God says, “Hey, stop that,” it becomes a problem. Therefore, God knows this and wants to place us not only in a hierarchical relationship but also in an equal relationship, like that of heart and body.

First, He wants to make us sons, second, to become one, and third, to give us the creative power of God. Thus, humans desire to possess even what God rejoiced in when He created. All of you here, whether older or younger, have experienced that when parents have something good, everyone wants to possess it. They want to make it their own. In this view, what belongs to the father is considered to be mine.

Also, are there parents who wish to give birth to children who are inferior to them? Parents who have given birth to a child, even if that child is not attractive, would be happy if the child is more attractive than themselves. Even among Buddhas, when they give birth to their first or second child, they cherish that child, and the more attractive the child is, the more they say the child resembles them. (laughter)

From this perspective, if God is our Father, He would certainly not want to create children who are insignificant or incapable. God created humans to stand in an equal position with the omniscient and omnipotent God, so our conscience desires the highest things.

Humans who have lost their inherent value
Let’s compare God to an author and humans to a work. When you have created something with great care and it does not turn out as you thought, it feels bad. However, if it turns out to be better than you imagined, would anyone feel bad saying, “Hey, why did this turn out better than I thought?” Well-made things are cherished and carried around, whether during sleep or when fleeing during a war; it is human nature to want to love them. This is because we resemble God. Therefore, God must also feel this way.

From this perspective, if God, who is omniscient and omnipotent, has left us humans as we are, it cannot be that way. God is an omniscient and absolute being, so if God is pleased, humans must feel good, and if God speaks, humans must listen, and if God goes, humans must also be created as beings who can go with Him. Resolving World Problems and the Existence of God

When we look at today's world situation, we know that neither the democratic world nor the communist world can solve the quest for one world on their own. Principles of Existence and Action

We know that this universe exists. For existence, prior conditions are necessary. Existence cannot occur without action. Action leads to movement. Therefore, existence and action are inseparable and cannot be divided. Action cannot occur in isolation. There must always be a counterpart for action. The relationship between subject and object is an absolute factor.

If I were to raise and lower my hand alone, people would say, "That person is crazy." However, if I see something small hanging on a spider web going up and down while I raise and lower my hand, I cannot help but say that I am a normal person. If the President of the United States were to laugh loudly and give a lecture alone in such a large hall, everyone would judge that the President is not a normal person. However, if he places a cup or something smaller, like a little piece of paper, and speaks loudly while laughing, then the President at that moment is a normal person.

If there is an absolute God, and that God is laughing and dancing alone without any object, without the existence of a counterpart, we can conclude that even if He is an absolute God, He is not a normal God. However, if God is delighted and laughing and dancing over the smallest object, then He is a normal God. Existence must go through action to continue. You must recognize how important the relationship between subject and object is for existence.

If there are subjects and objects, actions that result in loss will never occur. The fact that you are here this evening is the same. You came to see what kind of person Mr. Moon is, but if you were completely aware that you would incur a loss, no one would be here. You came because you thought you might gain something by meeting Mr. Moon and hearing something from him. When you leave here this evening, if you think, "Oh, I shouldn't have come. I lost a lot," you will not come back even if invited again. Therefore, actions do not occur to incur losses. We cannot see actions continuing or existence persisting if they lead to losses.

In San Francisco, people often go out to Market Street. If someone goes out every day to incur a loss, that person would be considered crazy. People come and go there to gain something. When that place maintains a condition where everyone can benefit from each other, they will continue to enter and exit.

For subjects and objects to act, they must discover a common goal that benefits both. Otherwise, the action will cease. It means that there is no improvement, no progress, and no growth. If we establish a principle that the subject and object act to diminish, we conclude that this universe cannot be formed. However, from the standpoint of being able to discover more valuable content in mutual exchange, and being able to face a greater purpose, it is from this principle of acting toward a positive direction that the universe can be formed.

From this perspective, we can see that the principle of action requires an objective purpose for valuable results to manifest. This indicates that the universe must be connected to some absolute subject-object relationship.

Conscience Action Connects God and Humanity

Let us liken God to an author. When an author creates a work, they do so centered on their vision and purpose, and when the created work turns out better than they envisioned, they cannot abandon that work. If that work becomes a unique, unimaginable masterpiece on this earth, when they flee or relocate, they will first take that with them. This is the nature of humanity.

Now, if God created the universe, we reach the conclusion that God cannot be pleased, rejoice, or take any action without an object. Would an absolute God create minerals as objects? No. Not even plants? Not even animals. The highest position among animals is humanity. God must consider humanity. If there is an absolute God, and we ask kindergarten children who that God created as an object, they would undoubtedly answer "humans."

If God created humans as masterpieces, He would not create them to be unable to recognize their owner. If you were the author, and you told your created work, "Hey, go over there," and it responded, "Yes!" and went, and laughed together upon seeing something good, how proud would you be of that creation? Therefore, when God created a masterpiece, He must have wanted to create beings that could communicate thoughts and emotions.

This would automatically align with God's desired purpose, and it would not be possible to create beings that do not wish to be with God. If such an absolute being created humanity, the purposes of humanity and the absolute being cannot diverge. Humanity must ascend to the absolute being, and the absolute being must descend to humanity, so that there can be a direction for unity. Without a direction for humanity to unite with the absolute being, there is no way for our purpose as created beings to align with that of our Creator.

If God created humanity as masterpieces, then that masterpiece, wanting to conquer God and make Him its own, would God dislike that? The highest authority of humanity is to make God their own and to make the world their own, exercising the greatest authority. This is the desire of humanity. Without this desire, one cannot possess the authority of the absolute God or the absolute God Himself. You cannot deny this.
