The existence of God through the mystery of the human body.  
Humans have eyes. If we ask where these eyes came from, we would answer that they came from our ancestors, tracing back to our very first ancestor's eyes. Now, did these eyes know that there was land when they were born on Earth? Did they know there was a solar system? They did not know. The eyes did not know. However, the eyes were born like this.  
And when we look at the eyes, they blink. The reason the eyes blink is that if moisture evaporates due to the sun's radiation, it would be a disaster, so they blink to keep the moisture. Did the eyes know that they had to blink to prevent moisture from evaporating?  
Look at the eyebrows. The eyebrows seem insignificant, but they have created a screen because they knew there was dust in the air. Did the eyebrows know there was dust in the air? Did they know about sweat? They are designed this way to prevent sweat from dripping down.  
What if the nose were upside down? Why is it designed this way? The nose already knew it should not be upside down. The nose also knew there was dust in the air. Do you know why the nose widens as it goes down? It is because if water were to flow down into the mouth, it would be a disaster. Everything is like that.  
Why is the ear shaped this way? If it were upside down, it would be a disaster. It is designed to funnel sound waves into the ear canal, preventing disasters.  
The human body is a kingdom of mysteries. How many world-class doctors could emerge from this one body? It is a kingdom of mysteries that could produce countless doctors. No matter how loudly they boast, they are merely benefiting from the results. Thus, it must be swapped while being placed in such a position. When Jacob received the blessing from Isaac, who did what? Because the root of sin is in the mother, according to the principle of indemnity, the mother must cooperate with the son to have a way to become one with him; otherwise, they cannot return to God. Therefore, Rebecca held onto the younger son and cooperated to become one with him to return to God. Thus, she performed the act of swapping the firstborn. This is not a figurative story; it is stating a fact. Ultimately, Jacob deceived Isaac and deceived his father.

Eve deceived God the Father at the time of the fall. And Cain became aligned with the deceived mother. To indemnify this, just as Satan and Eve deceived God the Father, the mother and son deceived Isaac, who was in the position of God, by becoming one.

When Rebecca became pregnant with the twins Jacob and Esau, they struggled in her womb. So when Rebecca said to God, "The two children are struggling," God said, "Two nations are in your womb, and the older will serve the younger." Without swapping this, the principles of heaven cannot be established, so God informed Rebecca of this content.

Jacob was wise. He did not just take the birthright; he went hunting and, upon returning, gave hungry Esau lentil stew and bread, asking him to sell his birthright. Therefore, even if Esau tries to reclaim the birthright based on that condition, he has established conditions that Satan cannot accuse him of externally.

Thus, before the standard of cooperation between mother and son, Jacob received the blessing and stood in a position to receive God's love. Ultimately, when Abel offered his sacrifice and stood on God's side, Jacob found himself in the same position as Cain, who hated Abel, which is why Esau wanted to kill Jacob.

At that time, Jacob, with his mother's cooperation, went to find his uncle in Haran, enduring a path of suffering for 21 years. Thus, he received blessings and returned to his brother Esau after 21 years. Jacob received the promise of the birthright from Esau but did not have the actual power. Therefore, Jacob had to win in reality to possess the birthright. In that position, on his way back, Jacob wrestled with an angel by the Jabbok River all night and achieved victory.

Restoration of the Womb Centered on Perez and Zerah

What is the fall? It is when Adam is dominated by the archangel. Therefore, we must turn around what Adam was dominated by the archangel. We must win. Without determining the position of the victor, we cannot block the archangel's authority, that is, Satan. For this reason, Jacob said, "I will not return unless you set conditions to bless me," and fought with Satan all night. Eventually, after the angel struck Jacob's hip, he was finally blessed. This was because Adam misused his hip, and according to the principle of indemnity, after striking down what had fallen, the angel finally blessed him. Thus, Jacob appeared before Esau, the substantial object, with the authority of having defeated the spiritual angel. Here, Jacob offered everything to Esau, and instead of standing in the position of being killed by his brother Esau, he stood in a position of welcome. This restored the situation where Cain killed Abel in Adam's family. By subduing the angel who stood on the side of Satan and Cain, the basis for restoration was established, and the beginning of the Israelite nation started. From here, the way to return to God was finally opened.

However, the problem here is that although the swap was made, since it was done as adults, the swap could not reach the womb. The adults swapped here belong to the side of Satan, so they must be swapped again.

Therefore, centered on Judah, the son of Jacob, this act is performed again. Here, Tamar had to take a risk to fulfill her purpose and be prepared to sacrifice her life. Thus, Tamar deceived her father-in-law to receive twins. Knowing that if her pregnancy became known, she would be killed, Tamar risked death to continue the blessed lineage of God. Thus, Tamar became pregnant with twins.

When she gave birth, the firstborn, Zerah, extended his hand first, so the midwife tied a scarlet thread around his hand. This signifies that before the Lord comes, at the end of this world, communism will emerge. However, the older brother Zerah, who was supposed to come out first, was pushed aside by his younger brother Perez, who was born first. He was named Perez because he pushed aside his brother and was born first.

Perez was born with the foundation of victory to swap the birthright from Tamar's womb. By being born after pushing aside his brother Zerah from Tamar's womb, all the bloodline connections that had been crossed were properly established, and the tradition of Israel was established.

Thus, it concludes that Jesus must come from the tribe of Judah. This victorious foundation, inheriting the traditional thought of Israel, waits and develops until a nation is formed. Since the nation centered on the authority of evil dominates this world, Jesus must come as a nation of good authority that can stand above the nation of evil. From this standpoint, after going through 2,000 years of Israel's history, Mary finally conceived Jesus.

Jesus Born as the Son of God Without Original Sin

Everyone, the Bible states that the virgin Mary gave birth to Jesus. The question is, why did God have to have Jesus born through the betrothed Joseph and Mary? Adam and Eve were in a position similar to that of engagement until just before the fall. To explain this in more detail would take several hours, and since time has passed, I will briefly move on.

When we look at Joseph and Mary, Joseph is in the position of the archangel. Therefore, Joseph must absolutely obey Mary. Understanding this reveals the reason why Jesus had to die. The fall occurred because of the mother and son, so the mother of Jesus must act in unity with Jesus until they establish the nation and cooperate in finding the nation. This was the position of Mary.

Joseph brought Mary as God taught him, but I know there were many troubles regarding the question of who her husband was concerning the fact that Mary was pregnant. In that process, Jesus was born from Mary's womb.

Since Mary inherited the victorious traditional foundation that Tamar had purified, even though Jesus was born, Satan could not claim that that child received his blood. Thus, for the first time, a son whom God could love was born on this earth. Therefore, you must understand that Jesus could become the only begotten Son who could receive God's love.

When examining the contents of the Bible, there are events behind the scenes. What Mr. Moon is saying here is not fabricated. You cannot deny the facts as they are. You need to understand this.

Until now, Christians have not known this content. Since such love was born, there has only been one person throughout historical ages, making Jesus the one who stands at the highest position representing religion, and the one who can represent God's love and become the body of God. For this reason, although Jesus died, Christianity could not help but stand at the highest position before God's providence in this era, which is a natural conclusion when viewed from this principle.

Without grafting, we cannot find the way of God's sons, so we must clearly understand that a Messiah is absolutely necessary for fallen humanity.

Centered on one sovereignty, we must establish a nation stronger than the kingdom of Satan, a nation that God can govern, and without resolving original sin, we cannot become children of heaven and citizens of the heavenly kingdom.

Then, who do we believe in to believe absolutely? Adam fell because he did not absolutely believe. The one who comes to restore that is the Messiah. The Messiah is the person who completely believes before God, the one who has fully retrieved the body, and the one who has completely received love. Even if he faced hardships for 40 years in the Midian wilderness, he did not assimilate into the world of Satan and stood completely on God's side by absolutely believing without doubting God, which is why Moses received love from God.

John the Baptist is also the same. His parents and relatives would not have liked him going out to live in the wilderness.
